#version 300 es\n        #extension GL_OES_EGL_image_external_essl3 : enable\n        precision mediump float;\n\n\t\tin vec2 uvmask;\n        in vec2 uv;\n        out vec4 color;\n\n        const float DIV12 = 1. / 12.92;\n        const float DIV1 = 1. / 1.055;\n        const float THRESHOLD = 0.04045;\n        const vec3 GAMMA = vec3(2.4);\n\n        layout(location = 2) uniform samplerExternalOES tex0;\n\t\tlayout(location = 3) uniform float fFadeAmount;\n\t\tlayout(location = 4) uniform vec3 UniReserved1;\n\t\tlayout(location = 5) uniform vec4 UniReserved2;\n\t\tlayout(location = 6) uniform vec4 UniDitherOffsets;\n\n        void main()\n        {\n            vec2 realUv = vec2(uv.x, uv.y);\n\n            color = texture(tex0, realUv);\n\t\t\tmat3 _valve1_d2020d709 = mat3(\n\t\t\t\t1.04988847,  0.05442289,  0.00393458,\n\t\t\t\t-0.04433306, 0.96052738, 0.01122383,\n\t\t\t\t-0.005557,   -0.01509698,  0.98628952 );\n\t\t\tcolor.rgb = _valve1_d2020d709 * color.rgb;\n\t\t\t//color.rgb += fract(UniDitherOffsets.a * .43 + UniDitherOffsets.rgb + gl_FragCoord.x * 1.67 + gl_FragCoord.y * 1.127 ) * .00292;\n\t\t\tcolor.rgb *= fFadeAmount;\n
#version 300 es\n        layout (location = 0) in vec3 vertexPosition;\n        in vec2 vertexUv;\n\n        out vec2 texCoord;\n        void main() {\n            gl_Position = vec4(vertexPosition, 1.0);\n            texCoord = vertexUv;\n        }\n    
#version 300 es\n\nconst float gridSize = 100.0;\n\nconst float gridMinPixelsBetweenCells = 2.0;\n\nconst vec3 pos[4] = vec3[4](\n\tvec3(-1.0, 0.0, -1.0),\n\tvec3( 1.0, 0.0, -1.0),\n\tvec3( 1.0, 0.0,  1.0),\n\tvec3(-1.0, 0.0,  1.0)\n);\n\nconst int indices[6] = int[6](\n\t0, 2, 1, 2, 0, 3\n);\n\nlayout(location = 0) uniform mat4 p;\nlayout(location = 1) uniform vec2 cameraPosition;\nlayout(location = 3) uniform mat4 mv;\n\nout vec2 fragUv;\nout vec3 vViewDir;\nout vec4 vPositionWs;\n\nvoid main() {\n\tint idx = indices[gl_VertexID];\n\tvec3 position = pos[idx] * gridSize;\n\n\tposition.x += cameraPosition.x;\n\tposition.z += cameraPosition.y;\n\tvPositionWs = vec4(position, 1.0);\n\n\tvViewDir = vec3( inverse( mv ) * vec4(position.xz, -1.0, 0.0) );\n\tgl_Position = p * vec4( position.xz, -1.0, 1.0 );\n\tfragUv = position.xz;\n}\n   
#version 300 es\n        out vec2 uv;\n        layout(location = 12) uniform float group;\n        layout(location = 13) uniform float mode;\n        void main() {\n            uv = vec2(gl_VertexID & 1, gl_VertexID >> 1);\n            // Position based off of 0..1, 0..1\n            vec2 vPos = (uv - 0.5) * 2.;\n            vPos.y *= -1.0; // Flip image.\n            gl_Position = vec4(vPos, 0, 1);\n\n\t\t\t// Output UV over the actual area used.\n\t\t\tif( mode > 1.5 )\n\t\t\t{\n\t\t\t\t// Do nothing\n\t\t\t\tuv.y = (uv.y + group * .5) * 0.5 - .25;\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\telse if( mode > 0.5 )\n\t\t\t{\n\t\t\t\t// 2x2\n\t            uv.y = (uv.y + group*0.5) * 0.5 - 0.25;\n\t\t\t\tuv.x = uv.x * 0.5;\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\telse\n\t\t\t{\n\t\t\t\t// 4-way\n\t\t\t\tuv.y = (uv.y + group) * 0.25;\n\t\t\t}\n        }\n    
#version 300 es\n        out vec2 uv;\n\t\tout vec2 uvmask;\n        layout(location = 12) uniform float group;\n        layout(location = 13) uniform float mode;\n        void main() {\n            uv = vec2(gl_VertexID & 1, gl_VertexID >> 1);\n            // Position based off of 0..1, 0..1\n            vec2 vPos = (uv - 0.5) * 2.;\n            vPos.y *= -1.0; // Flip image.\n            gl_Position = vec4(vPos, 0, 1);\n\n\t\t\tuvmask = uv;\n            // Output UV over the actual area used.\n\t\t\tif( mode > 1.5 )\n\t\t\t{\n\t\t\t\tgl_Position = vec4( 0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 1.0 );\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\telse if( mode > 0.5 )\n\t\t\t{\n\t\t\t\t// Two-by-Two\n\t\t\t\tuvmask = uv * vec2( 1.0, 0.25 );\n\t            uv.y = (uv.y + group*0.5) * 0.5;\n\t\t\t\tuv.x = uv.x * 0.5 + 0.5;\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\telse\n\t\t\t{\n\t\t\t\t// 4-Square\n\t\t\t\tuvmask = uv * vec2( 1.0, 0.25 );\n\t            uv.y = (uv.y + group) * 0.25;\n\t\t\t}\n        }\n    
#version 300 es\nprecision highp float;\nout vec4 out_FragColor;\nlayout(location = 2) uniform float flFadeAmount;\n\nlayout(location = 4) uniform float flTime;\n\nin vec3 vViewDir;\n\nfloat osmooth( float t )\n{\n\treturn t * t * (3.0 - 2.0 * t);\n}\n\nfloat oosmooth( float t )\n{\n\treturn osmooth( osmooth( t ) );\n}\n\n// Original code MIT License...\n// Copyright (c)2014 David Hoskins.\nvec3 hash33(vec3 p3)\n{\n\tp3 = fract(p3 * vec3(.1031, .1030, .0973));\n    p3 += dot(p3, p3.yxz+33.33);\n    return fract((p3.xxy + p3.yxx)*p3.zyx);\n}\n\nfloat fclamp( float v )\n{\n\tif( v < 0.0 ) v = 0.0;\n\tif( v > 1.0 ) v = 1.0;\n\treturn v;\n}\n\nvoid main()\n{\n\tvec3 vViewDirNorm = normalize( vViewDir ) ;\n\tfloat azimuth = atan( vViewDirNorm.x, vViewDirNorm.z ) ;\n\tfloat lalt = length( vViewDirNorm.xz );\n\tfloat altitude = atan( vViewDirNorm.y, lalt );\n\n\tfloat vgrad = altitude / 3.14159 + 0.5;\n\n\n\tvec2 vdn2 = normalize( vViewDirNorm.xz );\n\n\tfloat bubbly = sin( cos( vdn2.x * 4.7 + flTime*0.628/2.0 ) +\n\tsin( flTime*0.628/5.0*0.0 + vdn2.y * 5.2 ) ) * 0.01;\n\n\n\tvec3 grad1 = vec3( 0.059, 0.31, 0.643 ) * 0.3 + vec3( 0.05 );\n\tvec3 grad2 = vec3( 0.027, 0.216, 0.486) * 0.2 + vec3( 0.025 );\n\n\tvgrad = oosmooth( oosmooth( oosmooth( vgrad + bubbly + 0.02) ) );\n\tvec3 color = vec3( mix( grad1, grad2, fclamp( vgrad  ) ) );\n\n\t// Dither to get rid of color bands.\n\tvec3 noise = hash33( vec3( gl_FragCoord.xy * 3.2, flTime*2.4 ) ) / 255.0;\n\tout_FragColor.rgb = color + noise;\n\n\tout_FragColor.a = flFadeAmount;\n}\n    
#version 300 es\n        precision highp float;\n\t\tlayout(location = 2) uniform float renderType;\n        layout(location = 3) uniform mat4 m;\n        layout(location = 4) uniform mat4 v;\n\t\tlayout(location = 1) uniform float length;\n\t\tlayout(location = 5) uniform float renderLine;\n\n\t\t// All of these are in view space.\n\t\tin vec4 vPointerPosDelta;\n\t\tin vec4 vPointerDirDelta;\n\t\tin vec4 vWorld;\n\t\tin vec4 vEyePos;\n\t\tin vec4 vHitPos;\n\n\t\tin float lineZ;\n\n\t\tout vec4 out_FragColor;\n\n        void main()\n        {\n\t\t\tif( renderType < 0.5 )\n\t\t\t{\n\t\t\t\tfloat fAlpha = smoothstep(0.2, 1.0, 1.f-lineZ);\n    \t        out_FragColor = vec4(0.67, 0.84, 0.9, fAlpha);\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\telse if( renderType < 1.5 )\n\t\t\t{\n\t\t\t\tfloat fAlpha = 0.8;\n    \t        out_FragColor = vec4(0.67, 0.84, 0.9, fAlpha);\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\telse if( renderType < 2.5 )\n\t\t\t{\n\t\t\t\t// AA Line.\n\t\t\t\t// With base of pointer at "0,0"\n\t\t\t\t//float fDistFromTargetOnSurface = vInternalPos.z + length;\n\n\t\t\t\tvec3 vRayFromEye = normalize( vWorld.xyz - vEyePos.xyz );\n\n\t\t\t\tvec3 n = cross( vRayFromEye, vPointerDirDelta.xyz );\n\t\t\t\tfloat rd = dot( n, vPointerPosDelta.xyz - vEyePos.xyz ) / length ( n );\n\t\t\t\tfloat oAlpha = 1.05-400.0*abs(rd);\n\n\t\t\t\t// From https://mathworld.wolfram.com/Line-LineIntersection.html\n\t\t\t\tvec3 x3 = vWorld.xyz;\n\t\t\t\tvec3 x4 = vEyePos.xyz;\n\t\t\t\tvec3 x1 = vHitPos.xyz;\n\t\t\t\tvec3 x2 = vPointerPosDelta.xyz;\n\n\t\t\t\tvec3 A = x2 - x1;\n\t\t\t\tvec3 B = x4 - x3;\n\t\t\t\tvec3 C = x3 - x1;\n\t\t\t\tvec3 C2 = x3 - x2;\n\t\t\t\tvec3 ABCross = cross( A, B );\n\n\t\t\t\t// Distance along pointer ray.\n\t\t\t\tfloat s = dot( cross( C, B ), ABCross ) / dot( ABCross, ABCross );\n\n\t\t\t\t// Distance from hand to point on ray.\n\t\t\t\tfloat s2 = dot( cross( C2, B ), ABCross ) / dot( ABCross, ABCross );\n\n\t\t\t\t// Distance along headset ray. (unsued)\n\t\t\t\t//float t =-dot( cross( C, A ), ABCross );\n\n\t\t\t\tif( s < 0.0 ) oAlpha = 0.0;\n\t\t\t\tfloat fLength = length( vHitPos.xyz - vPointerPosDelta.xyz );\n\t\t\t\tfloat closenessToNear = -1.0 - s2*80.0;\n\t\t\t\toAlpha = min( oAlpha, closenessToNear );\n\t\t\t\tif( renderLine < 0.5f) {\n\t\t\t\t\toAlpha = 0.f;\n\t\t\t\t}\n\n\t\t\t\t// Compute intersection with "ball" (or really flat circle) at intersection.\n\t\t\t\t// This is faster than a ray-sphere intersection.\n\n\t\t\t\tvec3 vecCircleHit = cross( vHitPos.xyz - vEyePos.xyz, vRayFromEye );\n\t\t\t\tfloat dotAlpha = 4.5 - 600.0*length( vecCircleHit.xyz );\n\t\t\t\toAlpha = max( dotAlpha, oAlpha );\n\n\t\t\t\tvec3 col = vec3( 0.3, 0.8, 0.7 );\n    \t        out_FragColor = vec4(col, max( 0.0, oAlpha ) );\n\t\t\t}\n        }\n
#version 300 es\n\t\tlayout(location = 0) in vec3 position;\n        layout(location = 0) uniform mat4 mvp;\n        layout(location = 3) uniform mat4 m;\n        layout(location = 4) uniform mat4 v;\n\t\tlayout(location = 1) uniform float length;\n\n\t\tout float lineZ;\n\t\tout vec4  vPointerDirDelta;\n\t\tout vec4  vPointerPosDelta;\n\t\tout vec4  vWorld;\n\t\tout vec4  vEyePos;\n\t\tout vec3  vInternalPos;\n\t\tout vec4  vHitPos;\n\n        void main() {\n\t\t\tvec3 scaledPos = position;\n\t\t\tscaledPos.xy *= 0.01;\n\t\t\tscaledPos.z = scaledPos.z * length;\n\t\t\tvHitPos = m * vec4( 0., 0., -length, 1.0 );\n\t\t\tvPointerDirDelta = m * vec4( 0.0, 0.0, 1.0, 0.0 );\n\t\t\tvPointerPosDelta = m * vec4( 0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 1.0 );\n\t\t\tvInternalPos = scaledPos;\n\t\t\tvWorld = m * vec4(scaledPos,1.0);\n\t\t\tvEyePos = inverse( v ) * vec4( 0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 1.0 );\n            gl_Position = mvp * vec4(scaledPos, 1.0);\n\t\t\tlineZ = abs(position.z);\n        }\n
